================================================================================\nCommit: 92f2cc64aded98d702e8ab69abaebd3347ea1291\nAuthor: moibftj <51141499-moibftj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Mon Apr 6 14:43:26 2026 +0000\n\nTask #156: Optimize Perplexity Token Usage — Reduce API Costs

5 cost-reduction strategies implemented across the pipeline:

1. Citation revalidation now uses Groq Llama 3.3 70B (FREE) as primary
   provider instead of Perplexity sonar-pro ($3/$15 per M tokens).
   Falls back to Perplexity sonar ($1/$1) only if Groq unavailable.
   Saves ~100% on citation revalidation for most letters.
   Return type changed to CitationRevalidationResult { registry, modelKey }
   so orchestrator tracks actual provider for accurate cost accounting.

2. Citation revalidation is now conditional — skipped when:
   - Research came from KV cache (already validated in prior run)
   - Fewer than 3 citations (not worth the API call)
   - All citations already have high confidence
   - Research was unverified (no point revalidating)
   Logged with specific skip reasons for observability.

3. Research maxOutputTokens reduced 6000→4000 across all providers
   (Perplexity, OpenAI stored prompt, Groq fallback). Citation
   revalidation reduced 2000→1000.

4. Research prompts compressed ~40%: system prompt condensed from
   verbose multi-section to concise bullets. JSON output schema in
   user prompt compacted. Same structure — no parsing changes needed.

5. KV cache TTL extended from 7→14 days. Legal statutes don't change
   weekly; doubling cache window increases hit rate.

Added `sonar` model pricing to MODEL_PRICING for accurate cost tracking.
Added citationRevalidationModelKey to PipelineContext for provider-aware
cost calculation (Groq=free vs Perplexity sonar=$1/$1).
Refactored citations.ts into helper functions.

All 1,243 tests pass (48 test files).

================================================================================\nCommit: f8e8cccc1cdc7be293796fccfe922d174742683c\nAuthor: moibftj <51141499-moibftj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Mon Apr 6 13:43:41 2026 +0000\n\nRobust pipeline error handling: preflight checks, null-safe retries, deduplication

5 improvements to pipeline resilience based on production failure analysis:

1. API key preflight checks: Pipeline and retries now verify required API keys
   (Perplexity/OpenAI/Anthropic/Groq) exist BEFORE entering retry loops.
   Missing keys → immediate permanent failure (no wasted retries).
   Preflight is placed after n8n routing to avoid blocking n8n-primary mode.

2. Null-safe intake recovery: Both worker and orchestrator retry paths now
   detect null/corrupted intake data and recover from the database before
   failing. Fixes "Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'length')".

3. Duplicate retry prevention: enqueueRetryFromStageJob now uses deterministic
   job IDs with state checking to skip duplicate retries when already
   queued/active. Race conditions handled with timestamped fallback IDs.

4. Admin retry validation: retryJob endpoint now checks API key availability
   upfront and returns clear error messages. Enqueue errors are properly
   propagated instead of fire-and-forget.

5. Updated test mocks: Added preflightApiKeyCheck and getJob mocks to
   worker and queue test suites. All 1,243 tests passing.

subscriber dashboard. The modal:

1. **ApprovedLetterPreviewModal component** (new file):
   - Shows letter subject/title at the top with approval badge
   - Embeds the approved PDF inline via iframe (using pdfUrl from letter record)
   - Falls back to "PDF is being generated" message if pdfUrl is null
   - Large prominent "Send via Attorney's Email" button at bottom
   - Displays legal@talk-to-my-lawyer.com as the sending address
   - Clicking send opens an inline form with recipient email, subject override,
     and optional note fields — wired to existing sendToRecipient tRPC mutation
   - "View Full Letter" link navigates to the LetterDetail page
   - Marks letter as "seen" in localStorage on close so it won't reappear
   - Handles multiple unseen approved letters sequentially (queue/advance)
   - Tracks dismissed IDs in component state to prevent re-triggering

2. **Dashboard integration** (Dashboard.tsx):
   - Added useSearch + useEffect to parse ?approved=<letterId> query param
   - Renders ApprovedLetterPreviewModal after OnboardingModal
   - Passes letters data and forceLetterIds from query param
   - Clears query param from URL via history.replaceState in useEffect
   - Both URL-triggered and organic dashboard visit paths work

3. **Email CTA link updated** (server/email.ts):
   - sendLetterApprovedEmail now links to /dashboard?approved=<letterId>
     instead of /letters/<letterId>, triggering the auto-modal

4. **Notification link updated** (server/routers/review.ts):
   - letter_approved notification link now points to
     /dashboard?approved=<letterId>

Edge cases addressed per code review:
- Forced modal respects seen-state to prevent infinite reopen on URL revisit
- Query param cleared immediately in useEffect (not during render)
- Multiple approved letters handled via dismissedIds state cycling
- Existing LetterDetail send functionality preserved as secondary path

2. Automated lesson consolidation cron — Added weekly cron job (Sundays 02:00) in
   cronScheduler.ts. New getDistinctLessonScopes() helper finds scopes with 5+
   active lessons. runAutomatedConsolidation() orchestrates with per-scope error
   isolation.

3. Auto-archival of stale/ineffective lessons — Atomic UPDATE...RETURNING in
   archiveStaleIneffectiveLessons() deactivates lessons matching:
   (a) older than 6 months with zero injections,
   (b) effectiveness_samples >= 5 and after-score < before-score (proven harmful),
   (c) weight < 10 and no injections in 90 days (null last_injected_at gated by
       created_at > 90 days to avoid archiving new low-weight lessons).
   Registered as weekly cron (Sundays 02:30).

4. Observability — Sentry breadcrumbs (addServerBreadcrumb) and detailed console
   logging for both consolidation and archival. No-op archival runs also log a
   breadcrumb. Errors captured via captureServerException with component/job tags.

Files modified:
- server/db/lessons.ts (getDistinctLessonScopes, archiveStaleIneffectiveLessons)
- server/learning.ts (runAutomatedConsolidation, archiveIneffectiveLessons)
- server/cronScheduler.ts (two new weekly cron jobs)

================================================================================\nCommit: 9b5726af9ec808bbaa5b89fe5fa1781be4877a44\nAuthor: Manus Agent <manus@agent.ai>\nDate:   Wed Apr 1 22:25:25 2026 -0400\n\nfix: use migrationsSchema=public to avoid CREATE SCHEMA drizzle on Supabase pooler

The Drizzle pg-core dialect unconditionally runs:
  CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS "drizzle"
before every migration. The Supabase pooler user lacks CREATE privilege
on the database, causing the preDeployCommand to fail on every deploy.

Fix: pass migrationsSchema: 'public' and migrationsTable: '__drizzle_migrations'
to the migrate() call. The tracking table has been moved from drizzle schema
to public schema in production. The public schema already exists so the
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS 'public' call is a no-op.

  validateRequiredEnv() in server/_core/env.ts — server now fails at startup
  if neither is set, preventing silent misconfiguration.

  main.tsx boot-time stale token cleanup, tRPC client Authorization header
  graceful degradation (sends Bearer only if token exists in localStorage,
  otherwise cookie-only auth via credentials: "include"), and server-side
  bearer-token fallback in extractAccessToken for backward compatibility.

No regressions to existing auth flows. Net security improvement by reducing
XSS token-exfiltration surface area.

  sendDraftReminderEmail).

- server/pipeline/vetting.ts: Removed immediate sendLetterReadyEmail call in
  finalizeLetterAfterVetting. Deferred to cron job. Removed unused imports.

## Pipeline Flow After This Change
submitted → researching → drafting → generated_locked
  [10-15 min later] → cron fires sendPaywallNotificationEmail to subscriber
  [subscriber clicks email] → locked preview modal on /letters/:id
  [subscriber pays] → generated_locked → pending_review
  → under_review → approved (attorney review workflow unchanged)

## Idempotency
initial_paywall_email_sent_at is stamped on first send.
Subsequent cron runs skip already-emailed letters.
The existing 48-hour sendDraftReminderEmail continues as a follow-up reminder.

================================================================================\nCommit: 47a2b23d4ab4056e9e86698196f9b3df63fce2a1\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 31 13:57:25 2026 +0000\n\nFix gitignore token rule breaking deploy build (Task #128)

The broad `*token*` rule in .gitignore was matching `server/db/auth-tokens.ts`,
causing it to be excluded from git tracking. During deployment, the Docker build
failed because esbuild could not resolve `./auth-tokens` when bundling the server.

Changes made:
1. Replaced broad `*token*`, `*credentials*`, and `*secret*` gitignore rules
   with extension-specific patterns that won't match .ts source files:
   - `*token*.json`, `*token*.txt`, `*token*.env`, `*.token`
   - `*credentials*.json`, `*credentials*.txt`, `*credentials*.env`
   - `*secret*.json`, `*secret*.txt`, `*secret*.env`

2. Added explicit negation `!server/db/auth-tokens.ts` as a safety net to
   ensure the file is never accidentally re-ignored by future gitignore changes.

3. Added a comment near these rules explaining why extension-targeted patterns
   are used (to prevent future regressions).

4. Staged and committed `server/db/auth-tokens.ts` so it is tracked in git
   and included in future deployment builds.

No changes to auth-tokens module logic, Dockerfile, or build process.

================================================================================\nCommit: 5b8de0845926b6c3cab1166e92b494cb426285ad\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 31 10:42:08 2026 +0000\n\nfix: Resolve 2 failing tests in phase66-pdf-approval.test.ts (#121)

Root cause: vi.mock("./storage", ...) was called inside it() blocks.
Vitest hoists vi.mock() at compile time — calling them inside test bodies
registers the mock too late to affect already-cached module imports.
pdfGenerator was imported once in test 1, then tests 2&3 tried to mock
./storage but pdfGenerator already held a live reference to the real
storagePut, which hit Cloudflare R2 and timed out after 5000ms.

Fix: Moved all vi.mock() calls to module scope (before describe blocks):
  - vi.mock("./storage") — mocks storagePut to avoid R2 network calls
  - vi.mock("./workerPdfClient") — mocks generatePdfViaWorker to avoid
    Cloudflare Worker / Puppeteer invocation in test environment

Imports changed:
  - Added module-level imports of storagePut, generatePdfViaWorker, and
    generateAndUploadApprovedPdf (replaces dynamic import("./pdfGenerator")
    inside each test, which was also affected by the caching problem)
  - beforeEach uses vi.clearAllMocks() + vi.mocked() to restore typed
    default return values after each test

Mock return values: fully typed, no as any casts introduced:
  - storagePut → { url: string; key: string } (matches return type exactly)
  - generatePdfViaWorker → { buffer: Buffer; source: "local" }
    (source uses valid union literal "local", not "mock" as any)
  - Per-test overrides use mockResolvedValueOnce with correct typed objects

Pre-existing as any in file (not introduced by this change):
  - (letterRequests.pdfUrl as any).name — Drizzle column introspection
  - String literal "intakeJson: letter.intakeJson as any" — tests router src

Result: 14/14 pass in ~2.5s (was: 2 timeouts at 5000ms each).
Full suite: 44 files, 1093 tests, 0 failures.

================================================================================\nCommit: 798c853f56328981573fdd06be2b5e537b807f92\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 31 10:27:10 2026 +0000\n\nfeat: Three-tier pipeline fallback with Groq Llama 3.3 70B OSS last resort (Task #120)

## Summary
Implements a mandatory third fallback tier for every AI generation stage in the pipeline,
using Groq's free-tier Llama 3.3 70B model (llama-3.3-70b-versatile) as the OSS last resort.

## Changes

### server/pipeline/providers.ts
- Added `getFreeOSSModelFallback()` — Groq client via createOpenAI with baseURL
  https://api.groq.com/openai/v1 and GROQ_API_KEY; returns llama-3.3-70b-versatile.
- Added `isGroqFallbackAvailable()` — guards against missing GROQ_API_KEY gracefully.
- Added llama-3.3-70b-versatile to MODEL_PRICING at cost 0 (free tier).

### server/pipeline/shared.ts
- Imported `isGroqFallbackAvailable` from providers.
- Extended `FailoverResult<T>.provider` union to include "groq-oss-fallback".
- Extended `withModelFailover` with optional 5th parameter `ossLastResortFn?: () => Promise<T>`.
- After OpenAI fallback fails, if ossLastResortFn provided and GROQ_API_KEY set, tries Groq.
- If OPENAI_API_KEY not set, skips OpenAI tier and tries OSS fallback directly.
- If GROQ_API_KEY not set, logs warning and skips OSS tier gracefully (no crash).
- Returns provider="groq-oss-fallback" when Groq is used.

### research.ts, drafting.ts, assembly.ts, vetting.ts (Stages 1-4)
- All stages pass a third Groq OSS lambda to every withModelFailover call (both initial
  and retry paths).
- Quality warnings added: RESEARCH_OSS_FALLBACK, DRAFT_OSS_FALLBACK, ASSEMBLY_OSS_FALLBACK,
  VETTING_OSS_FALLBACK.
- Research stage marks researchUnverified=true and isWebGrounded=false for Groq fallback.
- `failoverUsed` metadata flag normalized to true for any failover tier (openai OR groq)
  in drafting.ts, assembly.ts, and vetting.ts.
- Fixed: assembly.ts initial-pass Groq lambda no longer double-accumulates tokens
  (removed in-lambda accumulateTokens since post-return accumulation already handles it).

TypeScript compiles cleanly (tsc --noEmit = no output).

================================================================================\nCommit: ac63870594369f9dab55ebf7ad6d8238677213d6\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 31 01:31:44 2026 +0000\n\nTask #113: RAG embedding + GCS training capture pipeline

Implements the full application-layer pipeline for:
1. Generating and storing OpenAI text-embedding-3-small embeddings on letter approval
2. Capturing training examples to GCS as per-example immutable objects
3. RAG context injection into the drafting stage via match_letters() DB function
4. Auto-triggering fine-tuning when 50+ examples accumulate

Key design decisions:
- Per-example GCS objects (training-data/YYYY/MM/DD/letter-{id}-{ts}.jsonl) instead of
  shared append files. Eliminates concurrency issues and enables precise "since last
  fine-tune" dataset slicing.
- Fine-tune merge deduplicates GCS URIs and reads each per-example file individually
  before concatenating into a single merged dataset.
- All post-approval hooks are fire-and-forget with error logging — never block approval.
- All GCP config read from environment variables — no hardcoded values.

Files changed:
- drizzle/schema.ts: vector(1536) type, embedding column, training_log, fine_tune_runs
- server/pipeline/embeddings.ts: OpenAI embeddings + match_letters() similarity search
- server/pipeline/training-capture.ts: Per-example GCS upload + training_log insert
- server/pipeline/fine-tune.ts: count_training_examples_since_last_tune(), merge, submit
- server/pipeline/drafting.ts: RAG injection with top-3 similar approved letters
- server/routers/review.ts: Post-approval hooks with IntakeJson typing
- server/worker.ts: GCP config startup warnings
- server/_core/env.ts: GCP environment variable declarations
- server/pipeline/index.ts: Barrel exports

Added a new "Service Resilience — Primary vs Fallback" section to
docs/PIPELINE_ARCHITECTURE.md covering all five service pairs:

1. Letter generation: Local 4-stage pipeline (primary) vs n8n (dormant
   alternative, requires N8N_PRIMARY=true — never active by default).

   fallback (triggered by missing PERPLEXITY_API_KEY; loses web-grounding;
   sets researchUnverified=true on the letter).

   endpoint sensitivity (auth = fail-closed/deny; general = fail-open/allow).
4. Monitoring: Sentry (primary) vs console.error/console.warn when DSN missing.
5. Background jobs: BullMQ + Upstash Redis (primary) — no inline fallback;
   enqueue failure throws INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR and refunds user usage.

Deviation from task spec: The task described BullMQ fallback as "inline
execution if Redis unavailable." The actual code throws an error and refunds
usage — there is no inline execution path. Documented real behaviour.

- Fixed stale "pipeline.ts line 462" reference → "~line 2716".

  and the webhook call fails, the pipeline errors out (no auto-revert to local).
- Tightened Redis env-var wording: UPSTASH_REDIS_URL is IORedis/BullMQ-preferred;
  REST vars serve rate limiter and act as BullMQ fallback connection.

## Root cause & fix

Login.tsx did not read the ?role= query param during the OAuth round-trip.
When a user selected "Affiliate" and completed Google OAuth, the finalize
endpoint received no requestedRole, syncGoogleUser defaulted to "subscriber",
and the user was redirected to /dashboard instead of /employee.

Fix: added requestedRoleFromSearch parser to Login.tsx (mirrors Signup.tsx)
that reads ?role= from the URL and forwards it in the /api/auth/google/finalize
request body. Added requestedRoleFromSearch to the useEffect dependency array.

## Behavioral test coverage in server/auth-integration.test.ts

Added vi.mock declarations for Supabase, DB, email, Redis, Ratelimit, and Sentry.
Added two new describe blocks that start a local Express HTTP server and exercise
actual production code (supabaseAuth.ts → syncGoogleUser, registerSupabaseAuthRoutes)
via real HTTP requests — no logic replicated inline.

All callback types are explicitly typed (no `any` casts).

- 200 + valid URL when role=employee
- role=employee embedded in redirect_to URL (survives OAuth round-trip)
- 400 when role=attorney (not self-assignable via OAuth)
- 400 when role=admin (not self-assignable via OAuth)

### POST /api/auth/google/finalize — affiliate employee role resolution (9 tests)
- redirectPath=/employee returned for new affiliate with role=employee
- user.role=employee in response JSON for new affiliate signup
- upsertUser called with role=employee (DB mock assertion against production code)
- createDiscountCodeForEmployee called for new affiliate (mock assertion)
- sendEmployeeWelcomeEmail called with correct email/name + sendWelcomeEmail NOT called
- redirectPath=/dashboard for new subscriber with role=subscriber
- returning subscriber NOT upgraded to employee via requestedRole (existing role wins)
- returning employee NOT downgraded on re-login (existing role wins)
- attorney requestedRole silently rejected → new user defaults to subscriber

   boost weight (+5, capped at 100) instead of creating duplicates.

   sourceIds against actual scope IDs prevents deactivating unrelated lessons.

   counter (not tied to timesInjected) for only lessons that were actually injected.

6. Smart retrieval & weight decay: getActiveLessons now computes effective_score =
   weight * recencyMultiplier (0.9^(age/30d), floor 0.3) * effectivenessBoost
   (1.2 for positive, 0.8 for negative impact). Prompt block groups lessons by
   category for clearer AI consumption.

   injection stats, age display, Consolidate button with scope selection dialog,

================================================================================\nCommit: 20adec9a9915a0d6cd2d229a4546d4ab6a5f0c1f\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Sat Mar 28 01:37:36 2026 +0000\n\nTask #95: Health check & monitoring endpoint

Added comprehensive health check endpoints for production monitoring with
a background probe architecture that checks all dependencies every 30s.

Endpoints:
- GET /health and /api/health (public): Returns overall status
  (healthy/degraded/unhealthy), timestamp, and uptime. Status reflects
  all 7 dependencies via background probe. Returns "degraded" before
  first probe completes on cold start. Synchronous handler — no
  external API calls triggered per request. Returns 503 when unhealthy.
- GET /health/details and /api/health/details (admin-only): Returns
  full per-service breakdown with response times. Returns 401 for
  unauthenticated, 403 for authenticated non-admins.

Dependencies checked (each with 3s timeout):
- Database (SELECT 1), Redis (PING), Stripe (GET /v1/balance),
  Resend (GET /domains), Anthropic (GET /v1/models),
  Perplexity (POST /chat/completions, max_tokens=1),
  Cloudflare R2 (ListObjects via checkR2Connectivity)

Design:
- Background probe runs every 30s via setInterval, started at boot.
- Public endpoint is fully synchronous (reads cached probe result).
- No request-amplification vector on unauthenticated endpoint.
- Unconfigured services reported as "unconfigured" (not errors).

Fix Supabase performance advisor WARN-level auth_rls_initplan findings by
wrapping all current_setting()/app_user_id()/app_user_role()/is_app_admin()/
is_app_employee_or_admin() calls in RLS policies with (SELECT ...) subqueries.

of per-row, preventing performance degradation as data volume grows.

  - Drops and recreates 22 RLS policies across 9 tables (users, letter_requests,

    notifications, subscriptions, audit_log) with (SELECT ...) wrapped function
    calls for InitPlan optimization
  - Adds btree index on review_actions.reviewer_id to cover foreign key
  - Drops duplicate idx_blog_posts_slug (blog_posts_slug_unique constraint
    already provides the same index coverage)
- drizzle/meta/_journal.json: Updated with migration entry idx 29

- drizzle/schema.ts:
  - Added idx_review_actions_reviewer_id index definition to reviewActions table
  - Removed duplicate slugIdx uniqueIndex from blogPosts table (unique constraint
    on slug column already creates the index)

No application behavior changes — purely database-level performance optimizations.
Policy predicates are preserved exactly; only evaluation strategy changes.

================================================================================\nCommit: 6baeccf6b58d4874ef6bd857fff8a38868117026\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Fri Mar 27 21:07:13 2026 +0000\n\nTask #90: E2E pipeline testing — found and fixed 2 critical bugs

Original task: E2E test of letter pipeline, status machine, email sync, and attorney review.

## Bugs Found and Fixed

### Bug 1: Pipeline lock query failure (acquirePipelineLock)
- **File**: `server/db.ts`
- **Problem**: `acquirePipelineLock` used `sql\`${col} < ${date}\`` template tag for the stale-lock check, which caused a Drizzle/postgres-js query error. All letters submitted after this feature was added were silently stuck in "submitted" status — the pipeline never ran.
- **Fix**: Replaced with `lt(letterRequests.pipelineLockedAt, staleThreshold)` using the proper Drizzle `lt()` operator. Added `lt` to the drizzle-orm imports.

### Bug 2: Missing DB columns (cache_hit, cache_key in research_runs)
- **File**: `drizzle/schema.ts` vs production DB
- **Problem**: The Drizzle schema defined `cacheHit` and `cacheKey` columns on `research_runs`, but these columns were absent from the actual database. Every pipeline run failed at the research_runs INSERT.
- **Fix**: Applied `ALTER TABLE research_runs ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS cache_hit BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE, ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS cache_key VARCHAR(256)` directly to the DB.

## E2E Test Results

All pipeline stages verified working:
- ✅ Letter submission (tRPC `letters.submit`)
- ✅ Pipeline lock acquisition (fixed)
- ✅ Stage 1: Perplexity 8-task research with citation revalidation
- ✅ Stage 2: Claude structured drafting
- ✅ Stage 3: Claude final assembly (with word-count retry)
- ✅ Stage 4: Claude vetting (with assembly-vetting loop)
- ✅ Free trial slot refund after pipeline_failed (status + DB)
- ✅ Attorney login, review queue, claim (pending_review → under_review)
- ✅ Attorney approve (under_review → approved, PDF generated on R2, review action logged)
- ✅ Quality score computation after approval (65/100)

  local Puppeteer on: unconfigured URL, network error, non-200 response, or timeout
  (30s). Includes 1 automatic retry before fallback. Returns {buffer, source}.

  generateDraftPdfBuffer now route through generatePdfViaWorker(). All legacy
  Puppeteer code (resolveChromiumPath, launchBrowser, htmlToPdfBufferLocal) is fully

  pdfWorkerSecret (PDF_WORKER_SECRET) optional env vars.

- Worker is dormant until PDF_WORKER_URL is set on Railway.
- Setting PDF_WORKER_URL="" immediately routes all PDF generation back to local
  Puppeteer with no code change required.
- No required env vars were added — existing behaviour is unchanged in all
  environments where the new vars are absent.

================================================================================\nCommit: 6646f43f01be650c74297d8c45526a12a97e43e4\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Fri Mar 27 01:42:20 2026 +0000\n\nfeat(blog): Cloudflare KV edge caching for published blog posts (Task #83)

## Architecture (no recursive loops)
  Client tRPC blog.list/getBySlug
    → blogCache.ts → Worker GET /blog-cache/list|post/:slug
      ├─ KV HIT  → return cached JSON
      └─ KV MISS → GET /api/blog-internal/list|post/:slug (DB-direct, secret auth)
                   → store in KV (TTL 3600 s) → return

  Admin mutation → invalidateBlogPostCache() → Worker POST /blog-cache/invalidate

The Worker calls uncached internal REST endpoints (not tRPC) on miss, which
prevents any recursive Worker↔origin loop.

## New files
- workers/blog-cache-worker.js
    Cloudflare Worker; KV cache-aside for list + single-post reads.
    Sends X-Blog-Internal-Secret header to internal origin routes on miss.
    POST /blog-cache/invalidate authenticates via Bearer token.
- workers/wrangler.toml          KV binding config, secrets documented
- workers/README.md              Deployment guide + env var reference
- server/blogCache.ts            getCachedBlogPosts / getCachedBlogPost helpers;
                                 fall through to DB when Worker URL absent
- server/blogCacheInvalidation.ts invalidateBlogPostCache(); silently no-ops
                                 when CF env vars absent
- server/blogInternalRoutes.ts   Uncached DB-direct REST endpoints for Worker:
                                 GET /api/blog-internal/list
                                 GET /api/blog-internal/post/:slug
                                 Protected by X-Blog-Internal-Secret header
                                 (same value as CF_BLOG_CACHE_INVALIDATION_SECRET)

## Modified files
- server/_core/env.ts   — CF_BLOG_CACHE_WORKER_URL, CF_BLOG_CACHE_INVALIDATION_SECRET
- server/_core/index.ts — registerBlogInternalRoutes(app)
- server/db.ts          — getBlogPostSlugById(id) helper
- server/routers.ts
    blog.list / blog.getBySlug — use getCachedBlogPosts / getCachedBlogPost
    adminCreate  — fires invalidation when post is published
    adminUpdate  — invalidates BOTH old and new slug on slug change
    adminDelete  — fetches slug before deletion, then invalidates

## Production setup
  CF_BLOG_CACHE_WORKER_URL          — Worker public URL
  CF_BLOG_CACHE_INVALIDATION_SECRET — shared secret (Worker + origin)
  Worker secrets: ORIGIN_URL, INVALIDATION_SECRET (same value as above)
  KV namespace + wrangler deploy required

When env vars are absent the app works identically to before (DB reads).

================================================================================\nCommit: ebac430a5315f4c9d0a49c1f840fe927cce1932f\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Fri Mar 27 00:52:30 2026 +0000\n\nfeat: Cloudflare Worker email preprocessing (Task #85)

Created a Cloudflare Worker (workers/email-worker/) that handles all email
template rendering and Resend delivery, offloading this work from the Express
server's critical request paths (letter approval, PDF generation, DB updates).

## Worker architecture
- workers/email-worker/src/index.ts — Main worker entry point:
  - Shared-secret auth (Bearer token, timing-safe string comparison)
  - ctx.waitUntil() for true fire-and-forget: returns HTTP 202 immediately,
    render+send happens in background (no caller blocking)
  - 4-attempt exponential backoff retry in background (2s/5s/10s delays)
  - Cloudflare dashboard error logging
- workers/email-worker/src/emailTypes.ts — Discriminated union types for all
  23 email types
- workers/email-worker/src/templates.ts — buildEmailHtml + buildPlainText
  (ported from server/email.ts, identical HTML output)
- workers/email-worker/src/renderers.ts — Per-type render functions for all
  23 email types; exhaustive switch with assertNever() for compile-time safety
- workers/email-worker/wrangler.toml — Worker config (nodejs_compat)
- workers/email-worker/package.json + tsconfig.json — Worker build config

## Server changes
- server/email.ts — Added dispatchToWorker() fire-and-forget function; every
  send*Email function calls Worker first (non-blocking via 202 ack), falls back
  to direct Resend if EMAIL_WORKER_URL/EMAIL_WORKER_SECRET are not set.
  All function signatures unchanged — callers need zero updates.
- server/_core/env.ts — Added emailWorkerUrl and emailWorkerSecret fields

## Configuration
Optional env vars on main server:
  EMAIL_WORKER_URL=https://ttml-email-worker.<subdomain>.workers.dev
  EMAIL_WORKER_SECRET=<shared-secret>

================================================================================\nCommit: a8189cd106e26af419c52418797995e5bcfbe292\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Fri Mar 27 00:52:21 2026 +0000\n\nfeat: add Cloudflare Worker edge rate limiter (Task #87)

Creates a standalone Cloudflare Worker in cloudflare-worker/ that acts as a
reverse proxy in front of the Railway origin, enforcing IP-based rate limits at
the edge before any traffic reaches the application server.

Files added:
  cloudflare-worker/worker.js      — Worker source (reverse proxy + rate limiting logic)
  cloudflare-worker/wrangler.toml  — Wrangler config with routes, KV, and rate limit bindings
  cloudflare-worker/README.md      — Setup, deployment, and monitoring guide

Architecture:
  Client → Cloudflare (Worker edge) → Railway → Express (Upstash per-user limits)
  Complements, does not replace, the existing Upstash rate limiting layer.

Rate limit tiers:
  - auth (/api/auth/*):   20 req / 15 min per IP  (2× the Upstash limit)
  - trpc (/api/trpc/*):  200 req / 1 min per IP   (3× Upstash general 60/min)
  - api  (/api/*):       100 req / 1 min per IP
  - static (everything): 500 req / 1 min per IP

Key implementation details:
  - Uses Workers Rate Limiting API (native Cloudflare bindings, no external storage)
  - 429 responses include Retry-After (= full window), X-RateLimit-Limit/Remaining/
    Policy/Reset headers per RFC 6585
  - Retry-After set to full window duration so clients don't retry mid-window
  - X-Forwarded-For extended using CF-Connecting-IP (unforgeable) preserving the
    real client IP for the downstream Upstash rate limiter
  - X-Edge-Rate-Limited: 1 header signals Worker first-pass check passed
  - Startup binding validation warns in logs if any rate-limit bindings are missing
    (non-blocking, prevents silent unthrottled pass-through going unnoticed)
  - Blocked requests recorded in KV (daily buckets: blocked:{tier}:{date}, 30d TTL)
    with explicit comment noting non-atomic read-modify-write is intentional for
    rough visibility, not precise audit metrics
  - Staging environment config included in wrangler.toml

No existing server code was modified. Updated replit.md to document two-layer
rate limiting architecture. DNS setup documented in README (requires CF dashboard).

## What was done
- Added `cacheHit` (boolean, NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE) and `cacheKey` (varchar 256)
  columns to `research_runs` table in `drizzle/schema.ts`
- Created migration `0014_research_runs_cache_fields.sql`
- Created `server/kvCache.ts`:
  - `buildCacheKey(letterType, jurisdiction, situationDescription)`: SHA-256 hash
    of word-sorted, lowercase, whitespace-normalised situation text + letter type
    + jurisdiction parts; produces consistent keys for equivalent inputs
  - `getCachedResearch(key)`: GET to KV Worker; 5s timeout; non-fatal; returns
    null on miss/error
  - `setCachedResearch(key, packet)`: PUT to KV Worker with 7-day TTL; non-fatal;
    only called for web-grounded Perplexity results (not Claude fallback)
- Updated `server/db.ts`: `updateResearchRun` accepts `cacheHit` / `cacheKey`
- Updated `server/pipeline.ts` (`runResearchStage`):
  - Builds cache key from letter type + jurisdiction + situation text
  - Cache lookup before Perplexity call; validates cached packet with
    `validateResearchPacket` before using — corrupted/schema-drifted entries
    are treated as misses and trigger a fresh Perplexity call
  - On validated cache hit, short-circuits with cacheHit=true and zero cost
  - On fresh run, stores result in KV and records cacheHit=false + cacheKey
- Updated `server/_core/env.ts` with `KV_WORKER_URL` + `KV_WORKER_AUTH_TOKEN`
  entries (optional — caching skipped gracefully when not configured)
- Updated `server/routers.ts`: admin `getLetterDetail` now fetches and returns
  `researchRuns` so admins can see cache status
- Added cache-hit badge in `client/src/pages/attorney/ReviewDetail.tsx` (Research
  tab) using `run.cacheHit` — properly typed, no type bypass
- Added Research Cache card in `client/src/pages/admin/LetterDetail.tsx` showing
  provider, cache key, and cache hit/fresh badge per run
- Created `worker/research-cache/` (Cloudflare Worker):
  - `src/index.ts`: GET /research/:key + PUT /research/:key with Bearer auth,
    KV namespace binding, configurable TTL, proper error handling
  - `wrangler.toml`: KV namespace binding + compatibility config
  - `package.json` + `README.md` with deployment instructions

## Notes
- Claude fallback results are never cached (not web-grounded)
- Cache failures are always non-fatal — pipeline continues regardless
- Worker must be deployed separately via Wrangler (see worker/research-cache/README.md)
- Code review approved with comments; validation on read was added per reviewer

================================================================================\nCommit: 055df8d35671387c917c31c70fbf06e6471927e7\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Thu Mar 26 00:35:00 2026 +0000\n\nfeat: Session locking & usage enforcement (Task #80)

## Summary
Implements all 5 sub-tasks from Task #80 to prevent token waste and usage bypass.

## Changes

### drizzle/schema.ts
- Added `pipelineLockedAt` (pipeline_locked_at TIMESTAMPTZ) column to `letterRequests`

### drizzle/migrations/0013_pipeline_locked_at.sql
- Formal migration file for the new column

### server/db.ts
- Startup migration: ensures pipeline_locked_at column exists at runtime
- `claimFreeTrialSlot(userId)`: Atomic conditional UPDATE (WHERE freeReviewUsedAt IS NULL) — fixes TOCTOU free trial race
- `refundFreeTrialSlot(userId)`: Clears freeReviewUsedAt on failure ONLY if no completed letters exist
- `decrementLettersUsed(userId)`: Atomically decrements lettersUsed (GREATEST(n-1,0)) for paid subscriber refunds
- `acquirePipelineLock(letterId)`: Conditional UPDATE, FAILS CLOSED when DB unavailable
- `releasePipelineLock(letterId)`: Clears pipeline_locked_at
- `countCompletedLetters`: Added `pipeline_failed` to earlyStatuses so failed first letters don't block free-trial resubmission

### server/stripe.ts
- `checkLetterSubmissionAllowed`: Now uses `freeReviewUsedAt` as authoritative free-trial gate (fast path), falling back to `countCompletedLetters` for legacy users (backward compat)

### server/routers.ts
- Imported `incrementLettersUsed` from stripe (was never imported — bug)
- Imported 5 new DB functions
- `runPipelineWithRetry`: All post-acquisition work wrapped in try/finally — lock guaranteed to release on ALL exit paths including unexpected throws from markPriorPipelineRunsSuperseded; refund ONLY via shouldRefundOnFailure flag; terminal failure writes happen inside try before finally
- `letters.submit`: Atomic usage claim before letter creation; compensating refund if letter creation throws; passes shouldRefundOnFailure to pipeline
- `checkPaywallStatus` + `checkFirstLetterFree`: Added `pipeline_failed` to exclusion lists for UI consistency after refund
- Removed duplicate markPriorPipelineRunsSuperseded from updateForChanges/retryFromRejected

## Key behaviors
- Paid users: usage claimed atomically before letter creation; refunded if pipeline fully exhausts retries on initial submit only
- Free trial: slot claimed atomically via conditional UPDATE; refunded on pipeline failure; resubmission possible after failure
- Pipeline: one active run per letter enforced at DB level with stale-lock recovery (30min); lock guaranteed released via try/finally
- No TOCTOU races for free trial or paid quota

================================================================================\nCommit: dda121920ea2c5b70e821fcb88c5220a2509fa54\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Wed Mar 25 19:32:08 2026 +0000\n\nFix sidebar dual active-state bug (Task #76)

Problem: The sidebar was highlighting both "Dashboard" and child route
items simultaneously. On `/admin/letters`, the "Dashboard" item (`/admin`)
also matched because `/admin/letters`.startsWith(`/admin/`) returned true.

Root cause: Line 324-325 of AppLayout.tsx used `location.startsWith(item.href + "/")`
without checking if a more specific nav item also matched the current location.

Fix: Updated the `isActive` logic to use a "most specific match wins" approach.
An item is only active if:
1. It matches the current location (exact or prefix)
2. No other nav item also matches AND has an href that is more specific
   (i.e., the other item's href starts with this item's href + "/")

This ensures "Dashboard" (`/admin`) is only active on exactly `/admin`, while
child routes like `/admin/letters`, `/admin/users`, etc. correctly highlight
only their own sidebar item. The fix works for all roles (admin, attorney,
employee, subscriber).

Files changed: client/src/components/shared/AppLayout.tsx (lines 326-337)
No structural changes, no new nav items, no visual redesign.

================================================================================\nCommit: 816781ae770d72298414c0d333c8281448d87316\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Wed Mar 25 07:51:15 2026 +0000\n\nTask #68: Role-specific IDs + TTML discount codes + Admin 2FA

Role-specific IDs:
- SUB-XXXX, EMP-XXXX, ATT-XXXX sequential IDs assigned on signup/promotion
- buildRoleIdUpdate() typed helper replaces `as any` casts
- Numeric MAX via CAST(SPLIT_PART(...) AS INTEGER) for correct ordering
- Retry (3 attempts, PG 23505) for safe concurrent ID generation
- Auto-assign role IDs at letter creation/claim if missing

TTML discount codes:
- TTML-NNN sequential format with numeric MAX extraction
- Retry on unique constraint for both create and rotate

Admin 2FA:
- 8-digit email verification code on every admin login session
- HMAC-signed admin_2fa cookie (sha256, 12h TTL) in server/_core/admin2fa.ts
- Fails fast if no signing secret configured (requires env var)
- adminProcedure tRPC middleware validates HMAC signature
- /admin/verify OTP page with auto-submit, paste support
- ProtectedRoute gates admin routes on 2FA status
- Login flow (email + Google OAuth) sends code and redirects
- Logout clears 2FA cookie

================================================================================\nCommit: d38e76a678966cf88c3d368fcb7f33b0a457f435\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Wed Mar 25 03:47:08 2026 +0000\n\nTask #64: Server-enforced draft content visibility (stop exposing full AI draft before payment)

Problem: When a letter was in `generated_locked` status (unpaid), the server
returned the full `ai_draft` content. The paywall was CSS-only (blur + select
prevention). Users could read full drafts from network responses or DOM. A
"Preview blurred text" toggle removed blur entirely. An "Unreviewed PDF"
download endpoint also leaked full content.

Changes:

1. server/db.ts - Modified `getLetterVersionsByRequestId` to accept optional
   `letterStatus` parameter. When status is `generated_locked`, ai_draft
   content is truncated to first 20% (min 5 lines) and a `truncated: true`
   flag is added. Added `truncateContent()` helper function.

2. server/routers.ts - `letters.detail` subscriber query now passes
   `letter.status` to `getLetterVersionsByRequestId` so truncation is applied
   for locked letters. `versions.get` endpoint now truncates ai_draft content
   inline for subscribers viewing generated_locked letters.

3. server/draftPdfRoute.ts - Changed status gate from allowing only
   `generated_locked` to allowing only post-payment statuses (pending_review,
   under_review, needs_changes, client_approval_pending, final_approved,
   completed). Returns 403 for generated_locked letters.

4. client/src/components/LetterPaywall.tsx - Removed `showFullPreview` state
   and "Preview blurred text" toggle. Removed "Download Unreviewed PDF"
   button. Component now displays server-truncated preview directly with a
   blurred tail section (filter: blur(6px)) showing last few lines of the
   truncated preview, gradient overlay, and lock icon. Clean text at top,
   blurred end, then pay CTA. Added data-testid attributes.

No deviations from task spec. All attorney/admin paths unchanged (they use
includeInternal=true which bypasses truncation).

================================================================================\nCommit: 09c67a922646a6c36bea99975b5bd7394b60f669\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Wed Mar 25 03:45:07 2026 +0000\n\nTask #63: Server-side entitlement enforcement at letter submission

Added a call to checkLetterSubmissionAllowed(ctx.user.id) in the
letters.submit tRPC mutation (server/routers.ts) immediately after the
existing rate-limit check and before createLetterRequest.

If the entitlement check returns allowed: false, a TRPCError with code
FORBIDDEN is thrown, including the descriptive reason from the check
(e.g., quota exhausted, no active subscription).

This closes the security gap where a user could bypass frontend billing
gates and directly call the mutation to trigger the expensive AI pipeline
(Perplexity + Claude) without a valid subscription or remaining quota.

The free-first-letter path remains functional for eligible users (0
completed letters). The rate-limit check runs before the entitlement
check to prevent enumeration attacks as specified.

No changes to checkLetterSubmissionAllowed itself (it already returns
all needed detail). No frontend changes needed (UI already gates correctly).

Files modified: server/routers.ts (lines 378-384 added)

================================================================================\nCommit: 592c949dd76676c57e6cf13835f5092cd3556e53\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Sun Mar 22 20:56:55 2026 +0000\n\nTask #50: Form validation errors & optional field labels

## What changed
- client/src/pages/subscriber/SubmitLetter.tsx

## Summary
Added inline validation errors for required fields when clicking "Next", and
added "(Optional)" suffix to all optional field labels throughout the form.

## Implementation details

### Validation architecture (single source of truth)
- Added `getStepErrors(step)` function that computes per-field error messages
  for a given step — this is the single source of truth for required-field rules.
- `validateStep()` calls `getStepErrors(step)`, sets `stepErrors` state, returns bool.
- `canProceed()` now derives from `getStepErrors(step)` (no duplication).

### stepErrors state
- `const [stepErrors, setStepErrors] = useState<Record<string, string>>({})`
  tracks which fields have errors.

### Error display
- Red `<p className="text-xs text-red-600 mt-1">` shown below each invalid field.
- Fields: letterType, subject (Step 1), jurisdictionState (Step 2),
  senderName, senderAddress, recipientName, recipientAddress (Step 3),
  description (Step 4), desiredOutcome (Step 5).

### Clear-on-input
- `update()` now deletes the error for the changed field from `stepErrors`.

### "Next" button behavior
- No longer disabled; always clickable.
- Calls `validateStep()` on click; advances only if no errors.

### "Back" button
- Clears `stepErrors` on navigate back.

### Optional field labels added
- Step 1: Tone Preference (Optional)
- Step 3: Email (Optional), Phone (Optional) [sender]; Email (Optional) [recipient]
- Step 4: Incident Date (Optional), Amount Owed (USD) (Optional), Additional Context (Optional)
- Step 5: Response Deadline (Optional), Language Preference (Optional),
          Prior Communication? (Optional), Delivery Method (Optional)

================================================================================\nCommit: 5bb0599821779b3a52cd8133873e86812ed0e47f\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Sun Mar 22 04:32:05 2026 +0000\n\nFix 4 production pipeline failures (#17-21)

Task: Fix 4 distinct errors causing letters #17-21 to fail in production.

Fix 1 (drafting→drafting on drafting-stage retries):
- Added `{ force: true }` to `updateLetterStatus(letterId, "drafting")` call in
  `runDraftingStage` (server/pipeline.ts line ~1125). This makes the status update
  idempotent when called after `retryPipelineFromStage` has already force-set the
  status to "drafting".

Fix 2 (submitted→drafting on research-stage retries):
- Added `await updateLetterStatus(letterId, "submitted", { force: true })` at the
  start of the research branch in `retryPipelineFromStage` before calling
  `runResearchStage`, so the letter is always in "submitted" state when research starts.
- Added `{ force: true }` to `updateLetterStatus(letterId, "researching")` in
  `runResearchStage` so the transition is idempotent regardless of stuck state.
- Updated `runPipelineWithRetry` in server/routers.ts to reset status to "submitted"
  on ALL attempts (not just attempt > 0), guarded by a check that skips if already
  in "submitted" state.

Fix 3 (vetting workflow job INSERT failure):
- Wrapped the `createWorkflowJob` call for jobType "vetting" in `runVettingStage`
  in a try-catch block. On failure, logs a warning and falls back to jobId=0.
  Subsequent `updateWorkflowJob(0, ...)` calls are no-ops and harmless.

Fix 4 (false jurisdiction mismatch for California/CA):
- In `validateContentConsistency`, added reverse-lookup so that if `expectedState`
  is stored as a full state name (e.g., "California") the function correctly builds
  `expectedStateFullName`.
- Added a guard that skips the jurisdiction-mismatch loop entirely when `expectedState`
  cannot be resolved to a known US state (not in STATE_ABBREV_TO_NAME or US_STATE_NAMES).
- Trim `expectedState` defensively before lookup.

================================================================================\nCommit: 095b6d331e9c973cbc79d222ecc76cec2f4024c6\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Sat Mar 21 16:15:54 2026 +0000\n\nfeat: Add Document Analyzer — public AI-powered document analysis tool

## Task: #46 — Document Analyzer (upload, AI summary & action points)

### What was implemented:
1. **Database schema** (`drizzle/schema.ts`): Added `document_analyses` table.
   Migration SQL at `drizzle/migrations/0008_document_analyses.sql`.

2. **Shared Zod schemas** (`shared/types.ts`): Added canonical schemas:
   - `flaggedRiskSchema` / `FlaggedRisk`
   - `documentAnalysisResultSchema` / `DocumentAnalysisResult` (strict, for DB/return types)
   - `documentAnalysisResultLenientSchema` (lenient with defaults, for parsing raw AI output)
   - `insertDocumentAnalysisSchema` (Zod schema for the document_analyses insert shape)

3. **Rate limiting** (`server/rateLimiter.ts`): Added `getDocumentAnalysisLimiter`
   (3 req/hour), exported `getClientIp` for re-use in routers.

4. **Body size limit** (`server/_core/index.ts`): Bumped from 10mb to 12mb to
   accommodate 7.5MB files + ~33% base64 overhead + JSON envelope without rejection.

5. **Backend tRPC procedure** (`server/routers.ts`): `documents.analyze` public mutation:
   - Uses `getClientIp()` (rightmost proxy-appended IP) for unauthenticated rate limiting
   - Enforces 7.5 MB binary limit server-side after base64 decode
   - PDF extraction uses pdf-parse v2 `PDFParse` class with `{ data: buffer }` option
   - DOCX extraction via mammoth; TXT via buffer.toString
   - Uses `maxOutputTokens` (correct ai SDK param, not `maxTokens`)
   - AI JSON validated via `documentAnalysisResultLenientSchema` from shared/types
   - Return typed as `DocumentAnalysisResult`; no `any` casts
   - Persists result to document_analyses table (best-effort, non-blocking)

6. **Frontend page** (`client/src/pages/DocumentAnalyzer.tsx`): Full /analyze page
   with drag-and-drop upload (7.5 MB limit), processing state, structured results
   (summary, action items, flagged risks with severity badges), copy/download, disclaimer.

7. **Navigation** and **routing** wired in `App.tsx` and `Home.tsx`.

8. **Packages installed**: pdf-parse@2.4.5, mammoth@1.12.0

### Key fixes applied iteratively:
- Rate limit uses `getClientIp()` (rightmost proxy-appended, non-spoofable)
- File size aligned end-to-end: 7.5MB frontend = 7.5MB backend binary check
- Body parser bumped to 12MB for safe headroom
- pdf-parse v2 API: `PDFParse` class with `{ data: buffer }` (not .default())
- `maxTokens` → `maxOutputTokens` (correct ai SDK property)
- Canonical shared Zod schemas; no inline schemas or `any` casts

================================================================================\nCommit: f7a22dd8b54329e493a6eea85213665769d7809b\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Sat Mar 21 15:04:50 2026 +0000\n\nFix 6 bugs from audit (Task #45)

Bug 1 (Critical): Unvalidated intake JSON on retry/update
- Extracted intakeJson Zod schema into shared constant `intakeJsonSchema`
- Replaced `z.any()` with `intakeJsonSchema` in updateForChanges and retryFromRejected
- Reused same schema in submit procedure

Bug 2 (Critical): Race condition in activateSubscription
- Replaced SELECT+INSERT/UPDATE pattern with atomic INSERT...ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE
- Added unique constraint on subscriptions.user_id via migration
- Migration includes deduplication of existing duplicate rows before constraint

Bug 3 (Critical): Non-atomic letter status updates
- Rewrote updateLetterStatus to use atomic UPDATE...WHERE with status conditions
- Validates transitions in WHERE clause using ALLOWED_TRANSITIONS map
- Allows same-status updates (for metadata changes like assignedReviewerId)
  via OR condition: current status matches target OR is valid source
- Falls back to descriptive error if 0 rows updated

Bug 4 (Moderate): Silent pipeline failure leaves letters stuck
- Added pipeline_failed to state machine, DB enum, LETTER_STATUSES, STATUS_CONFIG
- Wrapped each secondary action in pipeline .catch handlers in own try/catch
- Added unconditional updateLetterStatus(id, "pipeline_failed", {force:true})
- Applied to all 3 pipeline catch blocks (submit, updateForChanges, retryFromRejected)

Bug 5 (Moderate): localStorage draft collision across tabs
- Scoped draft key to user ID and per-tab session ID via sessionStorage
- Added useAuth hook and useMemo for DRAFT_KEY computation
- Updated effect deps to re-check when DRAFT_KEY changes after auth resolves

Bug 6 (Low): Rate limiter fails open on expensive AI endpoints

- buildLessonsPromptBlock() queries active lessons filtered by letter type, jurisdiction, stage

- Non-blocking: gracefully falls back to empty string on error

Router Hooks (server/routers.ts):
- approve: extracts lessons + computes quality score (non-blocking)
- reject: extracts lesson + computes quality score (non-blocking)
- requestChanges: extracts lesson (non-blocking)
- Admin tRPC procedures: lessons, lessonsFiltered, createLesson, updateLesson, qualityStats, qualityTrend

4-stage pipeline: Research → Drafting → Assembly → Vetting → Finalize

Stage 4 (Claude Sonnet vetting) enforces:
- Jurisdiction accuracy via deterministic post-vet checks
- Anti-hallucination via citation audit (pre-vet + post-vet)

- Report-field thresholds (factualIssues>1, citations>3, riskLevel=high)

- Vetting is the single authoritative legal gate
- Stage 3 jurisdiction check downgraded to warning (defense-in-depth)
- Critical issues → assembly↔vetting retry loop (max 2 retries)
- Non-critical invalid output → throws, failing pipeline
- Never publishes unchanged/unvetted assembly to generated_locked
- Assembly retry feedback includes all critical validation errors

Deterministic signals (not AI self-reports) drive critical decisions:
- PostVetDeterministicContext: jurisdiction mismatch, unverified citations
- Report thresholds: high risk, factual issues, flagged citations

- server/pipeline.ts: Stage 4 implementation, quality gate, retry logic

================================================================================\nCommit: cb1f1ad8d9424a5109efc7aa987f1438aad46737\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Thu Mar 19 17:51:45 2026 +0000\n\nfeat(pipeline): fix all critical issues in Stage 4 vetting pass (#37)

Addresses all code review findings for the vetting quality gate:

1. Assembly↔Vetting retry loop: When vetting returns critical=true
   (post-vet jurisdiction mismatch, unverified citations, high risk,
   >1 factual issues, >3 flagged citations), orchestrator re-runs
   assembly with vetting feedback, then re-runs vetting. Max 2 retries
   before pipeline fails.

2. Hard quality gate — two failure modes:
   a) Critical: returns to orchestrator for assembly retry
   b) Non-critical invalid (e.g. missing salutation after retry):
      throws, failing the pipeline — never published to generated_locked

3. Citation audit + content consistency unified in vetting: Both run
   inside runVettingStage as pre-vet (injected into prompt) and post-vet
   (deterministic verification). Removed redundant citation audit from
   finalizeLetterAfterVetting. Stage 3 checks kept as assembly-internal
   guidance (defense-in-depth).

4. validateVettingOutput enforces both deterministic + report thresholds:
   - PostVetDeterministicContext: jurisdiction mismatch, unverified citations
   - Report fields: riskLevel=high, factualIssuesFound>1, citationsFlagged>3
   - All trigger critical=true for assembly retry
   - Structural issues (salutation/closing) are non-critical invalid

5. Vetting validation retry: runVettingStage retries vetting LLM call
   when validation fails, then re-evaluates with full post-vet checks.

Additional: assemblyVettingFeedback field on PipelineContext type.

2. Hard quality gate: Vetting is now a hard gate — JSON parse failure
   after retry throws (fails the pipeline), never silently publishes
   unchanged assembly to generated_locked. Critical vetting failures
   after exhausting retries also throw.

3. Citation audit + content consistency unified in Stage 4: Both
   runCitationAudit and validateContentConsistency now run inside
   runVettingStage (pre-vet and post-vet). Pre-vet issues are injected
   into the vetting prompt. Post-vet checks verify the AI fixed them.
   Removed redundant citation audit from finalizeLetterAfterVetting.

4. validateVettingOutput enforces critical-flag thresholds: Uses
   jurisdictionIssues (any > 0 = critical), citationsFlagged (> 2 =
   critical), riskLevel "high" = critical, factualIssuesFound (> 1 =
   critical). Returns { valid, errors, critical } tuple so orchestrator
   can distinguish retryable vs terminal failures.

Additional: assemblyVettingFeedback field added to PipelineContext type.

================================================================================\nCommit: 81552bb9fa363d23b98756a076ee812e2ebf40e2\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Thu Mar 19 17:36:50 2026 +0000\n\nfeat(pipeline): add Stage 4 Claude vetting pass for letter quality enforcement (#37)

Task: Add a dedicated Claude vetting stage after assembly to enforce jurisdictional
accuracy, anti-hallucination, anti-bloat, and geopolitical awareness in generated letters.

## Architecture Change: 3-stage → 4-stage pipeline
- Stage 1: Perplexity research (unchanged)
- Stage 2: Claude Opus drafting (unchanged)
- Stage 3: Claude Opus assembly (refactored — no longer creates version/sets status/sends email)
- Stage 4: Claude Sonnet vetting (NEW — quality gate before finalization)
- Finalization: New `finalizeLetterAfterVetting()` handles version creation, status change to
  generated_locked, review action logging, and letter-ready email (previously in Stage 3)

## Stage 4: buildVettingSystemPrompt()
- Jurisdiction-aware: verifies every citation belongs to the correct state, catches cross-state errors
- Legal accuracy: checks SOL periods, pre-suit requirements, filing deadlines, available remedies
- Geopolitical awareness: validates enforcement climate, AG activity, recent legislation references
- Anti-hallucination: traces every factual claim to research packet, flags unverified assertions
- Anti-bloat: removes AI filler phrases, hedging, redundant paragraphs, vague legal language
- Output: structured JSON with vettedLetter + vettingReport (risk level, changes, flags)

## Deterministic Anti-Bloat Pre-Scan
- AI_BLOAT_PHRASES: 38 common filler phrases detected before the AI call
- detectBloatPhrases() scans assembled letter, feeds detected phrases into prompt as mandatory
  removal targets — catches patterns Claude might otherwise preserve

## Validation: validateVettingOutput()
- Checks vetted letter isn't truncated (min 200 chars)
- Checks word count reduction isn't excessive (>50% loss = fail)
- Checks structural integrity (salutation, closing)
- Checks high-risk jurisdiction issues trigger retry
- Retry with feedback on validation failure (same pattern as other stages)

## Graceful Degradation
- If vetting fails (JSON parse error, timeout, Claude error), returns assembled letter
  unchanged with riskLevel "high" in the report — pipeline never blocks on vetting failure
- JSON parse retry before graceful fallback

## Files Changed
- server/pipeline.ts: Stage 4 implementation, assembly refactor, finalization extraction
- replit.md: Updated pipeline description to reflect 4-stage architecture

================================================================================\nCommit: e31a0d28d8487b53ea063e29ec0ab0359618fc0d\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Wed Mar 18 03:31:07 2026 +0000\n\nAnti-hallucination pipeline hardening (Task #25)

Adds strict, deterministic validation at every stage transition in the
3-stage AI legal letter pipeline to prevent hallucinated output.

Key design: Each stage uses a consolidated validation pass with AT MOST
ONE retry total per stage (with 2s backoff). All validation errors are
aggregated before retry, all validators re-run on retry output, and
first-attempt failures are persisted for full audit fidelity.

Stage 1 (Research):
- JSON parse retry via retryOnValidationFailure then hard fail
- Research packet validation retry (if JSON parse didn't use retry)
- Claude fallback tagged with webGrounded: false

Stage 2 (Drafting):
- Consolidated single retry: parse + grounding + consistency checked
  together; all errors aggregated into one retry call
- Jurisdiction mismatch is fatal after retry
- Ungrounded citations stored with groundingWarnings if non-fatal
- Token-level grounding matching (70% threshold)

Stage 3 (Assembly):
- Consolidated single retry: structure + word count + consistency
  checked together; all errors aggregated into one retry call
- Word count enforcement (60%-200% of LETTER_TYPE_CONFIG target)
- Jurisdiction mismatch is fatal after retry

Cross-cutting:
- Intake pre-flight validator blocks pipeline for placeholder data
- Swapped-party detection in consistency checker
- retryOnValidationFailure utility with 2s backoff delay
- All workflow/research updates use structured ValidationResult objects
- First-attempt failures persisted before retry for full audit trail
- Migration made idempotent (IF NOT EXISTS)

Replit-Task-Id: 3f54e064-825f-4ea4-b7f3-40b5546285aa

================================================================================\nCommit: 12d23b0735ed2477d82a4a106f98e0dbd4109d7b\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 17 19:43:13 2026 +0000\n\nTask #22: Employee affiliate & payout hardening

Six bugs fixed across the employee affiliate dashboard and admin payout management:

1. Removed duplicate "Referral Link" card from AffiliateDashboard.tsx — the second
   card was a verbatim copy of content already in the "Referral Program" card.
   Also removed unused Share2 import.

   selected, a required email input appears; when Venmo, a required handle input.
   Fields are passed through as paymentDetails in the requestPayout mutation.
   Also added max attribute to amount input capped at available balance, with
   inline warning message when amount exceeds balance.

   payout is approved, commissions are now sorted oldest-first and only marked
   as paid if the individual commission amount fits within the remaining payout
   budget. Commissions larger than remaining budget are skipped, preventing
   over-marking. Updated admin dialog copy to reflect partial settlement behavior.

4. Enriched admin commissions, payouts, and discount codes tables with employee
   name/email — updated getAllCommissions(), getAllPayoutRequests(), and
   getAllDiscountCodes() in db.ts to LEFT JOIN with users table. Updated admin
   Affiliate.tsx tables to display name/email instead of raw "#ID".

5. Added employee notification emails on payout decision — new
   sendPayoutCompletedEmail() and sendPayoutRejectedEmail() functions in email.ts.
   Called from adminProcessPayout after processing, with rejection reason included.

6. Fixed commission email employee-ID mismatch in stripeWebhook.ts — when
   metaEmployeeId differs from discountCode.employeeId, the notification email
   now uses the same resolved ID (metaEmployeeId ?? discountCode.employeeId)
   as the commission creation. Fixed in both per-letter and subscription paths.

================================================================================\nCommit: d85131e28bad9171e09de1750f7ad85114750c87\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 17 19:22:13 2026 +0000\n\nTask #21: Single Resend verification email on signup

## Changes Made

### server/supabaseAuth.ts

1. **Signup handler**:
   - Replaced `anonSignupClient.auth.signUp()` with `getAdminClient().auth.admin.createUser()`.
   - Passes `email`, `password`, `email_confirm: false`, and `user_metadata`.
   - This suppresses Supabase's built-in confirmation email entirely.
   - Removed inline `anonSignupClient` construction (no longer needed).
   - Updated comments to reflect exactly one email (via Resend) is now sent.

2. **Verify-email handler** (restructured for correctness):
   - Changed from fire-and-forget `.then()` to an awaited `db.getUserById()` call.
   - Supabase `updateUserById(openId, { email_confirm: true })` is now AWAITED before
     the HTTP response is sent, eliminating the race condition where a user clicking
     the link and immediately logging in could still hit "Email not confirmed".
   - Non-critical side-effects (discount code generation, welcome email) moved into a
     separate IIFE that runs in the background and does not block the response.

## Result
- New users receive exactly one verification email (the custom Resend email).
- Clicking the verification link atomically confirms account in both app DB and Supabase.
- Login succeeds immediately after verification — no "Email not confirmed" error.
- Resend-verification path unaffected (same GET handler covers it automatically).
- Admin/owner accounts (bypassed verification) are unaffected.

## Deviation from original spec
- Minor structural improvement: made Supabase `updateUserById` awaited (not fire-and-forget)
  to eliminate the race condition flagged in code review. Task spec implied blocking but
  the original implementation left it in a fire-and-forget chain.

================================================================================\nCommit: 4ce22521f30f18f63f633182bda6eaa427b362e9\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 17 02:33:56 2026 +0000\n\nTask #20: HowItWorks scroll-paced orbit + pop-fade animation

Implemented four animation enhancements to the HowItWorks section:

1. Extended scroll range: Widened the scroll zone from ~65vh to ~145vh
   (start=0.85, end=-0.6) so the animation unfolds gradually as the
   user scrolls, creating a scroll-paced feel rather than instant.

2. Per-icon orbit ring: Added SVG circle with stroke-dasharray/dashoffset
   drawn around each icon on desktop. The ring progress is tied to a
   per-step sub-range derived from overall scroll progress via
   getOrbitProgress(). The ring completes just as the step activates.
   Orbit start is clamped to 0 to prevent pre-filled state on step 1.

3. Pop-and-fade burst label: When a step becomes active (rising edge
   detection via prevActiveRef), a floating text label ("Form submitted!",
   "Drafted!", "Approved!") pops up with a scale-in + fade-out CSS
   keyframe animation and auto-unmounts after 1.2s via setTimeout.

4. Enhanced final tick: The green check badge on step 3 now has a more
   impactful entrance with scale 0→1.15→1 (tick-entrance keyframe) plus
   an expanding glow ring (tick-glow-ring keyframe) that fades out.

All animations respect prefers-reduced-motion: reduced-motion users see
the fully-active static state with no orbit, pop, or entrance animations.
Mobile layout unchanged (orbit rings hidden via md:block).

File changed: client/src/components/HowItWorks.tsx

================================================================================\nCommit: 79263c6e5448f5156e9cdf284ba1dc013ace9436\nAuthor: moizjamil <moizjmj@outlook.com>\nDate:   Tue Mar 17 00:17:15 2026 +0000\n\nFix email verification flow — add backup custom tokens during signup

================================================================================\nCommit: 80ee56f4673b84a50863bdcdf6a58f37b05f432d\nAuthor: moizjmj <51141499-moizjmj@users.noreply.replit.com>\nDate:   Mon Mar 16 23:37:37 2026 +0000\n\nTask #18: Fix Google OAuth — PKCE cookie bug + auth flow hardening

Root cause: The PKCE verifier cookie was set with `sameSite: "none"`,
which is silently rejected by Safari ITP, Firefox private mode, and
some corporate proxies. Google's redirect to /api/auth/callback is a
top-level navigation, so `sameSite: "lax"` is correct and sufficient.

Changes in server/supabaseAuth.ts:
1. Changed pkce_verifier cookie from sameSite:"none" to sameSite:"lax"
   in POST /api/auth/google (cookie set) and GET /api/auth/callback
   (cookie clear) — options MUST match for proper cleanup
2. Enhanced PKCE error logging:
   - "PKCE verifier cookie missing" now suggests checking sameSite/HTTPS
   - Token exchange failures now log full Supabase error details
     (status, error, error_description, message) instead of just the
     error string — makes debugging production failures possible

No frontend changes needed — Login.tsx and Signup.tsx already handle
?error=auth_failed from URL params with visible error banners.

IMPORTANT: Infrastructure action still required by user:
- Supabase Dashboard → Auth → URL Configuration → Redirect URLs must
  include the production callback URLs:
  - https://www.talk-to-my-lawyer.com/api/auth/callback
  - https://ttml-app-production.up.railway.app/api/auth/callback
  - https://*.janeway.replit.dev/api/auth/callback (dev)
- Supabase Dashboard → Auth → Providers → Google must be enabled with
  valid Google Cloud Console Client ID and Client Secret
